Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于可微分物理仿真的样本高效、鲁棒最优控制方法，用于装配运动规划，显著减少仿真步数，并通过精确二阶导数提升优化性能与真实世界成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统装配运动规划依赖大量物理仿真，效率低；亟需一种样本高效、能兼顾精度与鲁棒性的新方法。

Method: 构建提供二阶解析导数的可微分物理仿真；采用内点法启发的平滑技术使碰撞检测与接触求解可微；改进线性规划形式的碰撞检测并高效计算一、二阶导数；建立多场景轨迹优化问题以增强sim-to-real鲁棒性。

Result: 实验证明该方法在真实机器人上实现>99%的成功率；验证了平滑接触建模与鲁棒建模对成功率的关键作用；仿真中证实使用精确Hessian比常用近似更优。

Conclusion: 所提可微分最优控制框架在样本效率、优化精度和真实部署鲁棒性方面均优于现有方法，为复杂装配任务提供了实用可行的新范式。

Abstract: Efficient planning of assembly motions is a long standing challenge in the field of robotics that has been primarily tackled with reinforcement learning and sampling-based methods by using extensive physics simulations. This paper proposes a sample-efficient robust optimal control approach for the determination of assembly motions, which requires significantly less physics simulation steps during planning through the efficient use of derivative information. To this end, a differentiable physics simulation is constructed that provides second-order analytic derivatives to the numerical solver and allows one to traverse seamlessly from informative derivatives to accurate contact simulation. The solution of the physics simulation problem is made differentiable by using smoothing inspired by interior-point methods applied to both the collision detection as well as the contact resolution problem. We propose a modified variant of an optimization-based formulation of collision detection formulated as a linear program and present an efficient implementation for the nominal evaluation and corresponding first- and second-order derivatives. Moreover, a multi-scenario-based trajectory optimization problem that ensures robustness with respect to sim-to-real mismatches is derived. The capability of the considered formulation is illustrated by results where over 99\% successful executions are achieved in real-world experiments. Thereby, we carefully investigate the effect of smooth approximations of the contact dynamics and robust modeling on the success rates. Furthermore, the method's capability is tested on different peg-in-hole problems in simulation to show the benefit of using exact Hessians over commonly used Hessian approximations.

### [414] [Self-Imitated Diffusion Policy for Efficient and Robust Visual Navigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22965)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准扩散策略依赖模仿学习，易继承专家示范的次优性和冗余性，导致推理时需大量采样与后处理筛选，计算开销大、效率低。

Method: 提出SIDP框架：1）奖励引导的自模仿机制，让策略自我采样并选择高质量轨迹进行迭代学习；2）奖励驱动的课程学习以提升数据利用效率；3）目标无关探索增强轨迹多样性与鲁棒性。

Abstract: Diffusion policies (DP) have demonstrated significant potential in visual navigation by capturing diverse multi-modal trajectory distributions. However, standard imitation learning (IL), which most DP methods rely on for training, often inherits sub-optimality and redundancy from expert demonstrations, thereby necessitating a computationally intensive "generate-then-filter" pipeline that relies on auxiliary selectors during inference. To address these challenges, we propose Self-Imitated Diffusion Policy (SIDP), a novel framework that learns improved planning by selectively imitating a set of trajectories sampled from itself. Specifically, SIDP introduces a reward-guided self-imitation mechanism that encourages the policy to consistently produce high-quality trajectories efficiently, rather than outputs of inconsistent quality, thereby reducing reliance on extensive sampling and post-filtering. During training, we employ a reward-driven curriculum learning paradigm to mitigate inefficient data utility, and goal-agnostic exploration for trajectory augmentation to improve planning robustness. Extensive evaluations on a comprehensive simulation benchmark show that SIDP significantly outperforms previous methods, with real-world experiments confirming its effectiveness across multiple robotic platforms. On Jetson Orin Nano, SIDP delivers a 2.5$\times$ faster inference than the baseline NavDP, i.e., 110ms VS 273ms, enabling efficient real-time deployment.

Method: LG-Flow Policy将动作序列编码为时间正则化的潜在轨迹，在潜在空间中学习显式流模型；并引入几何感知点云条件建模与执行时多模态调制（如视觉线索）。

Result: 在仿真与真实机器人平台上，LG-Flow Policy实现近单步推理，显著提升轨迹平滑性与任务成功率，优于原始动作空间的流匹配基线，且远比扩散模型高效。

Abstract: Learning long-horizon robotic manipulation requires jointly achieving expressive behavior modeling, real-time inference, and stable execution, which remains challenging for existing generative policies. Diffusion-based approaches provide strong modeling capacity but typically incur high inference latency, while flow matching enables fast one-step generation yet often leads to unstable execution when applied directly in the raw action space.
  We propose LG-Flow Policy, a trajectory-level imitation learning framework that performs flow matching in a continuous latent action space. By encoding action sequences into temporally regularized latent trajectories and learning an explicit latent-space flow, the proposed approach decouples global motion structure from low-level control noise, resulting in smooth and reliable long-horizon execution.
  LG-Flow Policy further incorporates geometry-aware point cloud conditioning and execution-time multimodal modulation, with visual cues evaluated as a representative modality in real-world settings. Experimental results in simulation and on physical robot platforms demonstrate that LG-Flow Policy achieves near single-step inference, substantially improves trajectory smoothness and task success over flow-based baselines operating in the raw action space, and remains significantly more efficient than diffusion-based policies.

Method: 提出IRL-DAL框架：1）FSM专家控制器进行行为克隆初始化；2）融合环境信号与IRL判别器构建混合奖励；3）条件扩散模型作为安全路径规划器；4）可学习自适应掩码（LAM）动态调整视觉注意力；5）PPO微调策略；6）两阶段课程学习训练。

Result: 在Webots仿真中达到96%任务成功率，碰撞率降至0.05次/千步，显著优于现有方法，并展现出对危险场景的专家级应对能力。

Conclusion: IRL-DAL通过多模块协同设计，有效提升了自动驾驶策略的安全性、泛化性与鲁棒性，为端到端安全导航提供了新范式。

Abstract: This paper proposes a novel inverse reinforcement learning framework using a diffusion-based adaptive lookahead planner (IRL-DAL) for autonomous vehicles. Training begins with imitation from an expert finite state machine (FSM) controller to provide a stable initialization. Environment terms are combined with an IRL discriminator signal to align with expert goals. Reinforcement learning (RL) is then performed with a hybrid reward that combines diffuse environmental feedback and targeted IRL rewards. A conditional diffusion model, which acts as a safety supervisor, plans safe paths. It stays in its lane, avoids obstacles, and moves smoothly. Then, a learnable adaptive mask (LAM) improves perception. It shifts visual attention based on vehicle speed and nearby hazards. After FSM-based imitation, the policy is fine-tuned with Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO). Training is run in the Webots simulator with a two-stage curriculum. A 96\% success rate is reached, and collisions are reduced to 0.05 per 1k steps, marking a new benchmark for safe navigation. By applying the proposed approach, the agent not only drives in lane but also handles unsafe conditions at an expert level, increasing robustness.We make our code publicly available.

</details>


### [420] [End-to-end Optimization of Belief and Policy Learning in Shared Autonomy Paradigms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.23285)
*MH Farhadi,Ali Rabiee,Sima Ghafoori,Anna Cetera,Andrew Fisher,Reza Abiri*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出BRACE框架，通过端到端可微的贝叶斯意图推断与上下文自适应辅助决策联合优化，显著提升共享自主系统在目标模糊与环境约束下的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有共享自主方法依赖静态混合比例或分离目标推断与辅助决策，难以在非结构化环境中兼顾任务成功率与用户自主性。

Method: 提出BRACE（Bayesian Reinforcement Assistance with Context Encoding）框架，将贝叶斯意图推断与基于环境上下文和完整目标概率分布的协作控制策略联合建模，并支持端到端梯度传播；理论分析辅助水平应随目标不确定性降低、随环境约束增强而升高，并证明融合信念信息可带来二次期望遗憾优势。

Result: 在三类递进式实验（2D光标人机交互、机械臂非线性动力学、目标模糊与环境约束下的集成操作）中，相比IDA、DQN等SOTA方法，成功率达6.3%提升、路径效率提升41%；相比无辅助控制，成功率达36.3%、路径效率达87%提升。

Conclusion: 集成优化在复杂、目标模糊场景下收益最大，且具有跨机器人领域的泛化能力，推动了自适应共享自主的SOTA进展。

Abstract: Shared autonomy systems require principled methods for inferring user intent and determining appropriate assistance levels. This is a central challenge in human-robot interaction, where systems must be successful while being mindful of user agency. Previous approaches relied on static blending ratios or separated goal inference from assistance arbitration, leading to suboptimal performance in unstructured environments. We introduce BRACE (Bayesian Reinforcement Assistance with Context Encoding), a novel framework that fine-tunes Bayesian intent inference and context-adaptive assistance through an architecture enabling end-to-end gradient flow between intent inference and assistance arbitration. Our pipeline conditions collaborative control policies on environmental context and complete goal probability distributions. We provide analysis showing (1) optimal assistance levels should decrease with goal uncertainty and increase with environmental constraint severity, and (2) integrating belief information into policy learning yields a quadratic expected regret advantage over sequential approaches. We validated our algorithm against SOTA methods (IDA, DQN) using a three-part evaluation progressively isolating distinct challenges of end-effector control: (1) core human-interaction dynamics in a 2D human-in-the-loop cursor task, (2) non-linear dynamics of a robotic arm, and (3) integrated manipulation under goal ambiguity and environmental constraints. We demonstrate improvements over SOTA, achieving 6.3% higher success rates and 41% increased path efficiency, and 36.3% success rate and 87% path efficiency improvement over unassisted control. Our results confirmed that integrated optimization is most beneficial in complex, goal-ambiguous scenarios, and is generalizable across robotic domains requiring goal-directed assistance, advancing the SOTA for adaptive shared autonomy.

</details>

### [421] [Screen, Match, and Cache: A Training-Free Causality-Consistent Reference Frame Framework for Human Animation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22160)
*Jianan Wang,Nailei Hei,Li He,Huanzhen Wang,Aoxing Li,Haofen Wang,Yan Wang,Wenqiang Zhang*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需训练的三阶段框架FrameCache，用于提升长序列人像动画的时序连贯性与视觉稳定性，通过动态筛选、动态缓存和行为匹配实现参考帧的高效利用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人类动画生成中，建模长程依赖关系并保持帧质量仍具挑战；受人类利用历史观察理解当前动作的启发，提出无需训练的框架以提升时序一致性。

Method: 提出FrameCache框架，包含Screen（多维质量感知自适应筛选）、Cache（基于动态替换-命中策略维护参考池）和Match（提取行为特征进行运动一致的参考匹配）三个阶段。

Result: 在标准基准上显著提升时序连贯性与视觉稳定性，且可无缝集成多种基线模型；但效果依赖于基线的时间推理能力与真实-合成一致性。

Conclusion: FrameCache是一种通用、即插即用的增强方法，其有效性揭示了对基线兼容性与自适应缓存机制的进一步研究需求。

Abstract: Human animation aims to generate temporally coherent and visually consistent videos over long sequences, yet modeling long-range dependencies while preserving frame quality remains challenging. Inspired by the human ability to leverage past observations for interpreting ongoing actions, we propose FrameCache, a training-free three-stage framework consisting of Screen, Cache, and Match. In the Screen stage, a multi-dimensional, quality-aware mechanism with adaptive thresholds dynamically selects informative frames; the Cache stage maintains a reference pool using a dynamic replacement-hit strategy, preserving both diversity and relevance; and the Match stage extracts behavioral features to perform motion-consistent reference matching for coherent animation guidance. Extensive experiments on standard benchmarks demonstrate that FrameCache consistently improves temporal coherence and visual stability while integrating seamlessly with diverse baselines. Despite these encouraging results, further analysis reveals that its effectiveness depends on baseline temporal reasoning and real-synthetic consistency, motivating future work on compatibility conditions and adaptive cache mechanisms. Code will be made publicly available.

</details>


### [422] [HeatMat: Simulation of City Material Impact on Urban Heat Island Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22796)
*Marie Reinbigler,Romain Rouffet,Peter Naylor,Mikolaj Czerkawski,Nikolaos Dionelis,Elisabeth Brunet,Catalin Fetita,Rosalie Martin*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出HeatMat方法，利用街景图像和预训练的视觉-语言模型（VLM）补充OpenStreetMap数据，高分辨率估计城市建筑表面材料，并构建2.5D热传导模拟器，以高效分析各类城市材料对城市热岛（UHI）效应的独立影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统传感器数据（如卫星或实地站点）空间与时间分辨率粗糙，难以准确研究城市热岛效应；同时，真实城市中建筑材料（尤其是立面）的精细分布难以获取，制约了对材料个体热效应的定量分析。

Method: 1）利用街景图像和预训练视觉-语言模型（VLM）识别并补全OpenStreetMap中的建筑立面材料信息；2）将材料与几何信息编码为多层2D地图，表征城市垂直结构与材料特性；3）构建轻量级2.5D耦合热传递模拟器，支持多分辨率、随机访问的地表温度估算。

Result: HeatMat实现了仅依赖开放数据的城市级高分辨率材料建模；2.5D模拟器相较等效3D模拟获得20倍加速，同时保持足够精度用于UHI归因分析。

Conclusion: HeatMat为在真实城市中解耦分析建筑材料对UHI的影响提供了可扩展、高效且开源友好的新范式，弥合了遥感观测、材料普查与微气候模拟之间的鸿沟。

Abstract: The Urban Heat Island (UHI) effect, defined as a significant increase in temperature in urban environments compared to surrounding areas, is difficult to study in real cities using sensor data (satellites or in-situ stations) due to their coarse spatial and temporal resolution. Among the factors contributing to this effect are the properties of urban materials, which differ from those in rural areas. To analyze their individual impact and to test new material configurations, a high-resolution simulation at the city scale is required. Estimating the current materials used in a city, including those on building facades, is also challenging. We propose HeatMat, an approach to analyze at high resolution the individual impact of urban materials on the UHI effect in a real city, relying only on open data. We estimate building materials using street-view images and a pre-trained vision-language model (VLM) to supplement existing OpenStreetMap data, which describes the 2D geometry and features of buildings. We further encode this information into a set of 2D maps that represent the city's vertical structure and material characteristics. These maps serve as inputs for our 2.5D simulator, which models coupled heat transfers and enables random-access surface temperature estimation at multiple resolutions, reaching an x20 speedup compared to an equivalent simulation in 3D.

</details>


### [423] [Learning to Build Shapes by Extrusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.22858)
*Thor Vestergaard Christiansen,Karran Pandey,Alba Reinders,Karan Singh,Morten Rieger Hannemose,J. Andreas Bærentzen*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为文本编码挤出（TEE）的新型3D网格表示方法，将网格构建表达为面挤出序列，并利用大语言模型（LLM）生成或编辑3D网格，支持任意面数、天然生成流形网格，并可对已有网格进行编辑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于Transformer的3D生成模型难以保证流形性、面数受限，且缺乏类似人工建模的可解释性和可编辑性；需一种更自然、可控、可泛化的网格表示与生成范式。

Method: 定义TEE为面挤出操作的文本序列；将四边形网格分解为非自交面环（building blocks）；用这些环的重装配挤出序列微调LLM；通过LLM解码生成或编辑网格。

Result: 实现了高质量网格重建、新颖形状合成及现有网格的特征添加；生成结果天然为流形，面数任意，支持编辑操作。

Conclusion: TEE是一种语义清晰、结构合理、兼具生成与编辑能力的文本化3D表示，结合LLM展现出在3D内容创作中替代传统几何表示的潜力。

Abstract: We introduce Text Encoded Extrusion (TEE), a text-based representation that expresses mesh construction as sequences of face extrusions rather than polygon lists, and a method for generating 3D meshes from TEE using a large language model (LLM). By learning extrusion sequences that assemble a mesh, similar to the way artists create meshes, our approach naturally supports arbitrary output face counts and produces manifold meshes by design, in contrast to recent transformer-based models. The learnt extrusion sequences can also be applied to existing meshes - enabling editing in addition to generation. To train our model, we decompose a library of quadrilateral meshes with non-self-intersecting face loops into constituent loops, which can be viewed as their building blocks, and finetune an LLM on the steps for reassembling the meshes by performing a sequence of extrusions. We demonstrate that our representation enables reconstruction, novel shape synthesis, and the addition of new features to existing meshes.

</details>


### [424] [EAG-PT: Emission-Aware Gaussians and Path Tracing for Indoor Scene Reconstruction and Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.23065)
*Xijie Yang,Mulin Yu,Changjian Jiang,Kerui Ren,Tao Lu,Jiangmiao Pang,Dahua Lin,Bo Dai,Linning Xu*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出EAG-PT方法，结合2D高斯表示与路径追踪，实现支持编辑的物理一致渲染，兼顾几何细节与光照一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有辐射场方法（如NeRF、3DGS）视觉质量高但不支持光照编辑；基于网格的逆渲染物理准确但依赖高质量几何，难以用于真实室内场景。

Method: 提出Emission-Aware Gaussians and Path Tracing（EAG-PT）：（1）以2D高斯作为统一、传输友好的几何代理；（2）在重建中显式分离自发光与非自发光分量；（3）解耦重建（单次弹射优化）与渲染（多弹射路径追踪），提升编辑灵活性。

Result: 在合成与真实室内场景实验中，EAG-PT在编辑后生成比辐射场方法更自然、物理更一致的渲染结果，同时比网格基逆路径追踪保留更精细几何、避免网格伪影。

Conclusion: EAG-PT为室内设计、XR内容生成和具身AI等应用提供了兼顾物理真实性与编辑能力的新范式。

Abstract: Recent reconstruction methods based on radiance field such as NeRF and 3DGS reproduce indoor scenes with high visual fidelity, but break down under scene editing due to baked illumination and the lack of explicit light transport. In contrast, physically based inverse rendering relies on mesh representations and path tracing, which enforce correct light transport but place strong requirements on geometric fidelity, becoming a practical bottleneck for real indoor scenes. In this work, we propose Emission-Aware Gaussians and Path Tracing (EAG-PT), aiming for physically based light transport with a unified 2D Gaussian representation. Our design is based on three cores: (1) using 2D Gaussians as a unified scene representation and transport-friendly geometry proxy that avoids reconstructed mesh, (2) explicitly separating emissive and non-emissive components during reconstruction for further scene editing, and (3) decoupling reconstruction from final rendering by using efficient single-bounce optimization and high-quality multi-bounce path tracing after scene editing. Experiments on synthetic and real indoor scenes show that EAG-PT produces more natural and physically consistent renders after editing than radiant scene reconstructions, while preserving finer geometric detail and avoiding mesh-induced artifacts compared to mesh-based inverse path tracing. These results suggest promising directions for future use in interior design, XR content creation, and embodied AI.

</details>
